
SOV_mobilization_of_red_guard_desisions = {

	mobilization_of_red_guard_213 = {
	
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
	
		available = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_government = social_democracy
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = RUS
				original_tag = SOV
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_government = social_democracy
			}
			213 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = mob_red_guard_industrial_complex
						value = var:industrial_complex_level
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = mob_red_guard_arms_factory
						value = var:arms_factory_level
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
		cost = 5
		
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 213 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					size < 1
					state = 213
				}
				213 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = 0.005 }
			213 = {
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = var:industrial_complex_level }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = var:arms_factory_level }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = mob_red_guard_industrial_complex }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = mob_red_guard_arms_factory }
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 4 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 1 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 0 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 1 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 4 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 1 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 0 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_government = social_democracy
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = RUS
				original_tag = SOV
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_government = social_democracy
			}
			236 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = mob_red_guard_industrial_complex
						value = var:industrial_complex_level
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = mob_red_guard_arms_factory
						value = var:arms_factory_level
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
		cost = 5
		
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 236 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					size < 1
					state = 236
				}
				236 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = 0.005 }
			236 = {
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = var:industrial_complex_level }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = var:arms_factory_level }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = mob_red_guard_industrial_complex }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = mob_red_guard_arms_factory }
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 4 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 1 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 0 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 1 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 4 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 1 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 0 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mobilization_of_red_guard_239 = {

					size < 1
					state = 239
				}

				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {

		available = {
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_government = social_democracy
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = RUS
				original_tag = SOV
			}
			OR = {
				has_government = radical_socialism
				has_government = communism
				has_government = social_democracy
			}
			588 = {
				is_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = {
					check_variable = {
						var = mob_red_guard_industrial_complex
						value = var:industrial_complex_level
						compare = less_than
					}
					check_variable = {
						var = mob_red_guard_arms_factory
						value = var:arms_factory_level
						compare = less_than
					}
				}
			}
		}
	
		cost = 5
		
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 588 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					size < 1
					state = 588
				}
				588 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = 0.005 }
			588 = {
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = var:industrial_complex_level }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = var:arms_factory_level }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = mob_red_guard_industrial_complex }
				subtract_from_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = mob_red_guard_arms_factory }
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 4 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 1 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 0 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 1 }
				}
				
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 4 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 4 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 3 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 1 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 2 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp > 0 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	mobilization_of_red_guard_590 = {
	
		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war
	
		available = {

						compare = less_than
					}

			}
		}
	
		cost = 5
		
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 590 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					size < 1
					state = 590
				}
				590 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialism popularity = 0.005 }
			590 = {
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = 0 }
				set_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = 0 }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp = var:industrial_complex_level }
				add_to_temp_variable = { mob_red_guard_arms_factory_temp = var:arms_factory_level }

					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 5 }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 3 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes

					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 4 }

				else_if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex_temp > 2 } }
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					spawn_krasnoarmeyskaya_brigada_in_state = yes
					add_to_variable = { mob_red_guard_industrial_complex = 3 }

				else_if = {
